## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.40pt;color:#464846">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.72pt;color:#6d6e6c">2G04</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#6d6e6c">年推出</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#6d6e6c">犀二个设计相</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">当优雅</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">的高性能网络</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">编程框架</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">这么</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">多年深</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#7c7e7b">受工程</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">师的喜爱.洞套</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.60pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">的设亩</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#7c7e7b">桌理和实</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#6d6e6c">跋藉华将有助于开发人员提</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">升网格编程水</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.65pt;color:#6d6e6c">平和中间件</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">设计水平</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">本书结合</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">源码解构及实际案例运用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">将与通信相关的知识逐一呈现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.59pt;color:#7c7e7b">非常值</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#464846">得</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">阅读</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#464846">作者</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#6d6e6c">在工作中一步一步把</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">应用在公司的许多关键服务的通信层上</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.07pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#6d6e6c">这些服务的稳定</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#6d6e6c">高效都得益于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">本身的强大与作者对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#6d6e6c">的娴熟</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">本书不仅汇聚了作者多年的实践经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.02pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#464846">还</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">展示了业界的知名开源案例中应用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.80pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">的经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#6d6e6c">本书可以帮助初学者深入理解和应用好</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.60pt;color:#464846">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:6.57pt;color:#464846"> o</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">几年前</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#7c7e7b">我在设计一个端到端的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">DevOps</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.74pt;color:#7c7e7b">自动化软件开发框架时</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">关于使用的关键组件</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:3.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">在国内几乎找不</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">到参考资料</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">本书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">作者帮助我知其然</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.97pt;color:#6d6e6c">知其所</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#7c7e7b">以然</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.74pt;color:#7c7e7b">本书融合了</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#6d6e6c">作者十余年一</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.88pt;color:#6d6e6c">线开发经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.32pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">作者善于将复杂问题简单化</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#7c7e7b">本书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#6d6e6c">有助于</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#7c7e7b">读者轻松掌握</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:16.60pt;color:#6d6e6c">刖</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.50pt;color:#595b58">为什么会写</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">这本书</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.50pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#7c7e7b">目前已成为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">Java</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#7c7e7b">网络编程领域热门的框架</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:6.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#6d6e6c">是开发</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#7c7e7b">者构建高性能</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Java</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.87pt;color:#7c7e7b">服务器</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#6d6e6c">的重要</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">框架</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.13pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#6d6e6c">不仅包含丰富</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#7c7e7b">的网络</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">知识</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.52pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#6d6e6c">还蕴</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">含很多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">Java</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">编程</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">的高阶技巧</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">是学习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">Java</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#6d6e6c">网络编</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">程的经典</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.95pt;color:#7c7e7b">框架</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#595b58">然而</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#595b58">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.86pt;color:#6d6e6c">目前市面上系统研究</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#595b58">的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#6d6e6c">资料并不多</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#6d6e6c">己有的资料要么强调通过源码解析原</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">理</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.87pt;color:#7c7e7b">要么侧重如何应用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.07pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.87pt;color:#7c7e7b">表造成了以下现象</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">：</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#7c7e7b">一方面</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.07pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">读者学完</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#7c7e7b">源码后</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.04pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">可能对</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.45pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">的具体实现很了解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">但是往往不明</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#6d6e6c">白所学的知识</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#7c7e7b">该如何</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.89pt;color:#6d6e6c">应用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">；</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">另一方面</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#7c7e7b">读者可能熟悉</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#595b58">的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">使用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">但往往停留在</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.39pt;color:#7c7e7b">“</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">人云亦云</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.17pt;color:#7c7e7b">”</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">的阶段</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.61pt;color:#6d6e6c">对源</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.85pt;color:#7c7e7b">码不够了解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">一旦出现问题就无从下手</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">；</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">而</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.89pt;color:#595b58">更</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#6d6e6c">多读者面临的困境是源码懂</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#7c7e7b">一些</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#6d6e6c">实践会一些</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.80pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.66pt;color:#6d6e6c">但是</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#595b58">完全不</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.65pt;color:#6d6e6c">知道自己的理解或运用是否合理</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:3.71pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#6d6e6c">原因主要在于他们完全不知</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#7c7e7b">道业界</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#6d6e6c">的最佳实践是什么</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#595b58">我</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">在学习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">的过程中</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#7c7e7b">也曾遇</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">到过以</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">上困境</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.99pt;color:#6d6e6c">它们也是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">开发人</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#6d6e6c">员面临的共性问题</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">通过梳理自己的学习</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">过程和经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.15pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">我发现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.13pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">如果读者能围绕一个网络应用案例程序的开发来学</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.20pt;color:#595b58">习</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty,</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.87pt;color:#7c7e7b">就很容</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.58pt;color:#6d6e6c">易建立</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">起自己的知识体系</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.49pt;color:#7c7e7b">明白</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#6d6e6c">所学知识如何</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">运用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#7c7e7b">并借鉴业界主流</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.51pt;color:#6d6e6c">开源软</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#595b58">件中</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">方面</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.62pt;color:#6d6e6c">的使用经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">如此一</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">来</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.17pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">理解和应用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#595b58">何</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#6d6e6c">愁没有信心</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:5.85pt;color:#6d6e6c">？</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#595b58">基</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">于以上思路</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.98pt;color:#7c7e7b">恰逢机缘巧合</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#6d6e6c">结识了人民邮</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">电出版社的张涛老师之后</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">我决定写一</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.98pt;color:#595b58">本能够</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#7c7e7b">紧密结合理论和实际的书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#6d6e6c">以帮</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">助读者轻松</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">高效地掌握</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty,</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">这就是本书的写作</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">初衷</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.50pt;color:#6d6e6c">搴苗内</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:13.80pt;color:#595b58">容</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#595b58">本</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#6d6e6c">书是一本兼顾入门和进阶的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">指南</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">适合没有接触过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">或只具</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#595b58">备少量</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.17pt;color:#6d6e6c">使</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">在内</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.95pt;color:#7c7e7b">容上</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.32pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">本书以</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#7c7e7b">-个网络应用案例程序的开发作为主线</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.57pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#595b58">本</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">书分三部分</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#7c7e7b">包含</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">18</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">章和两个附录</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">第一</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">部分主要介绍什么是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.50pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.32pt;color:#6d6e6c">以</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.90pt;color:#7c7e7b">及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">的过去</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#7c7e7b">现状与发展趋势</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">重点阐述完成-个</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">简单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">应用程序所必备的基础知识</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">并从源码层面进行分析</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.40pt;color:#595b58">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.20pt;color:#595b58">1</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#6d6e6c">的角色和</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">功能</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">通过演示两个</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">简单的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">案例使读者建立初步印象</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#7c7e7b">同时</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:3.71pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.90pt;color:#595b58">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.50pt;color:#595b58">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.98pt;color:#6d6e6c">章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#6d6e6c">基础</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">知识</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">比如编译</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">代码的方式</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#6d6e6c">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#7c7e7b">常见</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">的编译问题</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#7c7e7b">案例</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">程序的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.80pt;color:#595b58">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.10pt;color:#595b58">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.64pt;color:#7c7e7b">章首先金国篡见的数据编码以及为网络应用程序选择数据编码的要点</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.27pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">然后讲述</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.44pt;color:#7c7e7b">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#595b58">对这</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.50pt;color:#6d6e6c">些数据编码液</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">jf</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">情况</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.13pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">并讨论常见开源软件对数据编码的选择</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.27pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#7c7e7b">最后讲述案例程序的数</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#595b58">据</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">编码的选择和实现,</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">也就是如何完成数据的第一层编码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.10pt;color:#595b58">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.60pt;color:#595b58">4</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.87pt;color:#6d6e6c">章首先介绍为什</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">么要对</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#6d6e6c">网络消息进行</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">定界以及常见的定界</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">方式</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.89pt;color:#7c7e7b">然后基于源码解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.70pt;color:#595b58">析</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#6d6e6c">对常见定界方式中的封帧</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.86pt;color:#7c7e7b">是如何进行支</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#6d6e6c">持的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">并</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">讨论常见开源</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#6d6e6c">软件对</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">封帧方案的选</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">带</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#7c7e7b">的文件</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.86pt;color:#8b8d89">应用作</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#7c7e7b">为案例来解析</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#8b8d89">关键实</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#7c7e7b">现点</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.40pt;color:#595b58">17</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.61pt;color:#6d6e6c">的一些不常用但经常让</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#7c7e7b">人津津乐道的特性</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.59pt;color:#7c7e7b">并且解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.63pt;color:#6d6e6c">析它们的源码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#7c7e7b">实现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:3.65pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">这些特性不</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.98pt;color:#7c7e7b">仅包括</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.86pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">对虚拟机内管道</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.46pt;color:#6d6e6c">(In-VM</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.30pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">pipe)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.60pt;color:#7c7e7b">和</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">UNIX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">域套接字</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">(Unix</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.30pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.29pt;color:#595b58">domain</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.30pt;color:#595b58"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.38pt;color:#6d6e6c">socket)</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#6d6e6c">的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">支持</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.86pt;color:#7c7e7b">还包括</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.98pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.82pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.00pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#6d6e6c">对</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.98pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.62pt;color:#6d6e6c">JDK</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:12.10pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.70pt;color:#7c7e7b">的增强</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">(如</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.83pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.45pt;color:#6d6e6c">FastThreadLocal</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.00pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.07pt;color:#7c7e7b">和</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.27pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.51pt;color:#7c7e7b">Hashed</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.70pt;color:#6d6e6c">WheelTimer).</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:11.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.50pt;color:#6d6e6c">18</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#7c7e7b">章从注解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#6d6e6c">使用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#6d6e6c">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.49pt;color:#6d6e6c">内存</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#7c7e7b">使用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">多线程并发</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">开发流程</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.32pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#8b8d89">代码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">规范这</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.60pt;color:#7c7e7b">5</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.58pt;color:#7c7e7b">个方面介绍使用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#7c7e7b">便于读者将这</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#8b8d89">些经验</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">应用到自己的项目实</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#8b8d89">践中</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:5.02pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">附录</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">A</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.47pt;color:#7c7e7b">列出了</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.45pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.77pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">TCP</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">通信</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">支持的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#7c7e7b">实现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.52pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#7c7e7b">附录</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.60pt;color:#6d6e6c">B</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">列</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.66pt;color:#8b8d89">出了本</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">书中一</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#8b8d89">些重要</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">术语的翻译</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">为</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">了兼顾入门和进阶</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.98pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.61pt;color:#6d6e6c">本书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.51pt;color:#595b58">解析了</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#595b58"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.30pt;color:#595b58">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.65pt;color:#7c7e7b">中大量的代</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.86pt;color:#8b8d89">码片段</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.13pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.49pt;color:#8b8d89">还借鉴了</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.77pt;color:#8b8d89"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.59pt;color:#7c7e7b">Cassandra</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:7.86pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.65pt;color:#7c7e7b">Dubbo</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.52pt;color:#7c7e7b">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">Hadoop</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.95pt;color:#7c7e7b">等常用开源软件的代码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#8b8d89">实现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#7c7e7b">以</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#8b8d89">寿助读者深入理解</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#8b8d89">学以致用</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.40pt;color:#6d6e6c">配套资源</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#595b58">本书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">的配套资源托管参见</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.46pt;color:#595b58">https://github.com/jiaful</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:7.82pt;color:#595b58"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.30pt;color:#595b58">1</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.57pt;color:#595b58">15/netty-practice,</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.64pt;color:#6d6e6c">其中主要包</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#595b58">含以下</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">内容</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:5.02pt;color:#6d6e6c">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">□</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.94pt;color:#6d6e6c">带中文注释的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">Netty</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.96pt;color:#6d6e6c">源码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#6d6e6c">：</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.20pt;color:#6d6e6c">存放在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">sourcecode</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#7c7e7b">文件夹中</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">详解了更多细节</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.69pt;color:#6d6e6c">□</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#6d6e6c"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.89pt;color:#6d6e6c">实</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">战案例程序</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.41pt;color:#7c7e7b">：</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#7c7e7b">存放在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.91pt;color:#6d6e6c">example</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.81pt;color:#7c7e7b">文件夹中</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">其中包</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#8b8d89">含了本书所完</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#7c7e7b">成案例程序的</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#8b8d89">完整实</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#8b8d89"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#6d6e6c">现</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#7c7e7b">代码</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.70pt;color:#7c7e7b">致谢</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.20pt;color:#8b8d89">和声明</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.49pt;color:#8b8d89">完成一个项•日可能只</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.44pt;color:#7c7e7b">需要</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.27pt;color:#8b8d89">fl:</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#8b8d89">备充足的实战经验即可</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.13pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#8b8d89">但是</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.27pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.70pt;color:#8b8d89">把实战经验清晰地呈现给读者</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#8b8d89"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#7c7e7b">完全是另外一件事</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#8b8d89">对于我而言</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.20pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#8b8d89">这更是</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#8b8d89">--</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.65pt;color:#8b8d89">项</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.90pt;color:#7c7e7b">挑战</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.07pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#7c7e7b">因此</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">我只</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#8b8d89">能孜孜不倦</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.66pt;color:#8b8d89">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#8b8d89">诚</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">惶诚恐</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.59pt;color:#8b8d89">地以呈</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#8b8d89"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.72pt;color:#7c7e7b">现最好的内</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#8b8d89">容为目标来完成这项挑战</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#8b8d89">在此过程中</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.80pt;color:#7c7e7b">我</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#8b8d89">不得不感谢-•些热心的朋友</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.78pt;color:#7c7e7b">感谢</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#8b8d89">人民邮电出版社张涛老师的支持</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.76pt;color:#8b8d89">没有他对这一技术领域的关注</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.55pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#8b8d89">就没有本书</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.69pt;color:#8b8d89">；</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#8b8d89">没有</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#8b8d89"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.79pt;color:#7c7e7b">他的耐心和</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.84pt;color:#8b8d89">帮助</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.32pt;color:#8b8d89">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.74pt;color:#8b8d89">本书也不可能如此顺利地呈现在读者的面前</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.97pt;color:#7c7e7b">感谢&#x27;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.73pt;color:#8b8d89">&#x27;极客时间</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.45pt;color:#8b8d89">”</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.71pt;color:#8b8d89">的张浩</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.42pt;color:#8b8d89">、</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.74pt;color:#8b8d89">龚仕伟为本书提供的--些很好的建议</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#8b8d89">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.92pt;color:#6d6e6c">作</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">者权益的保护</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.30pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.74pt;color:#7c7e7b">也是我们持续为您提供有价值的内容的动力之源</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:4.77pt;color:#7c7e7b">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:14.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">关于异步社区和异步图书</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:6.75pt;color:#6d6e6c">“</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.10pt;color:#6d6e6c">异步社区&quot;</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.75pt;color:#7c7e7b">是人</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.67pt;color:#6d6e6c">民邮电</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.83pt;color:#7c7e7b">出版社旗下</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.60pt;color:#7c7e7b">IT</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.69pt;color:#7c7e7b">专业图书社区</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.93pt;color:#7c7e7b">，</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.82pt;color:#7c7e7b">致力于出版精品</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.62pt;color:#7c7e7b">TT</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#7c7e7b">图</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.55pt;color:#6d6e6c">书和相</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.31pt;color:#7c7e7b">关学习</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:9.50pt;color:#7c7e7b"> </span>
